 In 2014, the BJP was successful in winning 57 of these 64 seats
 is baar ke chunaav main sapa-basapa gathbandhan kar maidan main utari hai, jiske baad bijepi ko apni siten bachaae rakhane kii kadi chunauti he
 At the same time, elections to the 14 Lok Sabha seats of Jharkhand are to be held in the last four phases
 bijepi ne 2014 main 13 siten jeetne main safal rahi thi
 In this election, Congress and JMM have entered the electoral fray with many parties, in such a situation that their won seats are at stake for BJP
 bihar kii 40 loksabhaa siton main se 9 siton par voting ke baad ab bachi 31 siton par aagaamee paanch charnon main chunaav hone hai
 The BJP last won 22 seats
 is baar congress, argedy, araspi sahit tamaam dalon ke saath mahagathbandhan karke chunaav ranbhumi main utari he
 It is a big challenge for the BJP to maintain its dominance in Bihar
 iske alaava dilli kii saat or haryana kii 11 siton par chathe charan main voting honi he
 In 2014, the BJP was successful in winning all the seats in Delhi and then won 8 seats in Haryana
 is baar in donon rajyon kii siton ko bachaae rakhana aasaan nahin he
 All the four seats in Himachal Pradesh will be cast in the last phase of votes and in 2014 BJP won all these seats
 vahiin, pashchim bengal kii 42 siton main se 5 siton par chunaav ho chuke hai baaki bachi 37 siton par paanch charnon main vot daale jaaenge
 Apart from this, elections are also to be held in Odisha and Assam seats
 bijepi ko duusari baar satta main aane ke liye baaki paanch charnon ke chunaav kaaphi ahm maane ja rahe hai
 The BJP won 282 seats in the 2014 Lok Sabha elections, a gain of 166 seats compared to the 2009 election
 jabaki congress ko 44 siten mili jo ki 2009 kii tulana main 164 siton kaa nuksaan uthaanaa padaa tha
 In such a situation, the remaining elections in the remaining stages are no less than a litmus test for Prime Minister Narendra Modi and BJP President Amit Shah
 chunaav kii har khabar milegi sidhe aapke inbox main

 The proposal to remove Mistry was approved by the necessary majority in the company's shareholders' meeting
 tata samooh kii holding company tata sans ne ek bayaan main kaha, tata sans li
 The shareholders of the company voted in favor of the removal of Cyrus p Mistry from the post of directors with the necessary majority at an extraordinary general meeting of the company
 is ghatnakram kaa matlab he ki 10 saal main pehali baar shaporji pallonji parivaar kaa board main koi pratinidhitiv nahin hoga
 18 of Mistry's family in Tata Sons
 5 pratishat hissedari he
 Mistry joined the board of Tata Sons in 2006
 isse do saal pehle unke pita pallonji shaporji mistre ne nideshak pad se istipha de diya tha
 He was on the board of Tata Sons since 1980
 haalanki, mistre parivaar kii tata sans main 1965 se hissedari he
 Tata Sons had last month issued a notice calling for this extraordinary general meeting (EGM) to remove Mistry from the board of directors
 mistre ne is kadam kii vaidhata ko chunauti di thi
 The National Company Law Tribunal (NCLAT) last week turned down an appeal by two investment companies of Mistry's family to suspend EGM
 rashtriya company vidhi nyaayaadhikaran (ensielti) kii peeth ne 31 janvari ko koi raahat dene se inkaar kar diya tha jiske baad mistre khemaa ensieleti main gaya tha
 Tata Sons removed Mistry from the post of chairman on October 24 last year and proposed to be removed from his group business companies like Tata Sons and TCS
 24 aktubar, 2016 ko tata sans ne kaha tha ki mistre chairman pad se hatane ke baad bhi company ke nideshak bane rahenge
 Later issuing notice of the extraordinary general meeting of February 6, Tata Sons said that the relentless allegations made by Mistry on the Tata group had caused a lot of damage to the group
 aise main unka nideshak pad par bane rahane kaa koi auchity nahin banataa tathaa unhen is pad se hataaya janaa chahie
 Politics has been heated over allegations made by anti-corruption activist Arvind Kejriwal and his team against Robert Vadra, son-in-law of Congress President Sonia Gandhi
 bhartiya janata party (bhaajapa) va marxvaadi communist party (makapa) ne aaropon kii jaanch kii maang kii he vahiin dlef ne un aaropon kaa khandan kiya he jinamein kaha gaya he ki usne wadra ko phayda pahunchaaya or iske badale congressi rajya sarkaron se phaayde liye
 Kejriwal is still firm on the allegations that he had leveled against Congress President Sonia Gandhi's son-in-law Robert Vadra on Friday
 arvind kaa kahana he ki unhone kuch sachai janata ke saamne rakhi he, jiskaa jawaab aana jaruri he
 Meanwhile, DLF issued a statement saying that it did not give any loan to Vadra without security nor did he give any land at a cheap rate
 dlef ne kaha, "ham spasht karnaa chaahate hai ki dlef ne wadra ko bagaiyr suraksha raashi ke wadra ko yaa unki kisi bhi company ko koi rin nahin diya
 "according to him," at any stage the Skylight Group was not given any land at a cheaper rate than the amount offered to other customers
 " Kejriwal and his colleague Prashant Bhushan on Friday alleged that Vadra bought land in Gurgaon and other cities at a price below market price and made huge profits by selling them
 kejariwal ne kaha, "ham koi faisla nahin de rahe hai
 We have put some truth before the public
 vah (wadra) kyon inkaa jawaab nahin dete
 "he asked why DLF sold land worth Rs 35 crore to Vadra for just five crore rupees
 wadra ke gandhi parivaar se jude hone ke kaaran unhen nishaanaa banaae jane ke bare main puche jane par kejariwal ne kaha, "log is baat par sahamat nahin honge ki gandhi parivaar se jude hone ke kaaran hamane unhen nishaanaa banaaya
 "he said that we are neutral so the Congress and the Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP) have alleged that he is the agent of their opponents
 unhone kaha ki dlef or wadra ke sambandhon ke bare main iconomic times main chhapi khabar ko unhone padhaa nahin he phir bhi ek hi mudde ko phir se oochhaalane main koi nuksaan nahin he
 Union Finance Minister P
 chidambaram ne wadra par lage kathith aaropon ke maddenjar unka apratyaksh rup se bachaav kiya
 Chidambaram said in Mumbai that transactions between two private persons cannot be put under question on the basis of vague allegations of corruption
 chidambaram ne kaha, "ye aarope sahi hai yaa galat, mujhe iske bare main jaankaree nahin he
 Transactions between two private people cannot be put under question on the basis of vague allegations of corruption
 " Chidambaram said this when journalists asked him if the government would investigate the allegations against Vadra
 chidambaram ne haalanki yah bhi kaha ki unhen jo jaankaree mili he uske mutabik is lenden kaa iskar va anya vivaranon main zikr he
 On the other hand, the Congress on Saturday rejected the opposition's demand to investigate the allegations made by Arvind Kejriwal and Prashant Bhushan of India Against Corruption on Vadra
 kejariwal or unke sahyogi prashanth bhushan ne shuukravaar ko aarope lagaae the ki wadra ne gudgaanv or anya shaharon main bazaar bhav se kam keemat par jaminen kharidi or unhen bechakar baari munafa kamaaya

 gyaat ho ki bhaajapa or marxvaadi communist party (makapa) ne maamle kii jaanch kii maang kii he
 Gandhian social activist Anna Hazare has raised the demand for a judicial inquiry
 kejariwal dwaara wadra ko manahani kaa mukadmaa daayar karne kii di gai chunauti ke bare main puche jane par tiwari ne kaha ki congress ko aise vyakti kii salaah kii jarurat nahin he jo apni aage kii raajnneeti ke liye aaropon kaa sahaara le rahaa he
 The Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP) and the Communist Communist Party of india-marxist (CPI-M) have demanded an inquiry into the allegations, while the DLF has denied the allegations stating that it benefited Vadra and took advantage of Congress state governments in return
 kejariwal un aaropon par abhi bhi adig hai jo unhone shuukravaar ko congress adhyaksh sonia gandhi ke damaad robert wadra par lagaae the
 Arvind says that he has put some truth in front of the public, which needs to be answered
 is bich, dlef ne ek bayaan jari kar kaha ki usne wadra ko bagaiyr suraksha raashi ke koi rin nahin diya or na hi saste dar par unhen koi jameen di

" " uske mutabik, "kisi bhi str par skylite samooh ko anya graahakon ko di gai prastaavit raashi ke mukaable saste dar par koi jameen nahin di gai

 Born in Karnataka as an influential campaign to eradicate manual scavenging in India, Bejwada Wilson and Chennai singer TM Krishna were selected for the prestigious Ramon Magsaysay Award for the year 2016
 is puraskaar ke liye do bharatiyon ke alaava chaar anya ko chunaa gaya he jinamein philippine ke konchita carpiyo-morells, indonesia ke dompet duapha, japan oversij kooparation walantier evam laos ke ‘‘viyantien resecue’ shaamil hai
 Wilson, the national convener of the Safai Karmachari Andolan (SKA), has been nominated for the award "due to his steadfast talk of the right to live with human dignity" and to bring "social inclusiveness in culture" to Krishna
 Has been selected for the award under the "emergent Leadership" category
 wilson ke uddhran main kaha gaya he, ‘‘mailaa dhonaa bharat main maanviyata par kalank he
 Scavenging is the task of hand-lifting human excreta from dry latrines and carrying basins of excreta to the designated settlement sites in view of the structural inequality that India's "untouchable", Dalits have with them 
 ’ "scavenging is a hereditary profession and 1,80,000 Dalit households clean 7,90,000 public and individual dry toilets across India, 98 per cent of women and girls in scavengers," said 50-year-old Wilson's commendable mention
 Is paid a very nominal salary
 samvidhan evam anya kanoon shushk shauchalayon or logon se mailaa dhone par pratibandh lagaate hai lekin inhen lagu nahin kiya gaya he kyonki sarkaar hi inaki sabase badi ulanghankarta he
 Wilson was born into a Dalit family who used to do scavenging in Kolar Gold Fields town in Karnataka
 vah ucch shiksha praapt karne vaale apane parivaar ke pehle sadsy hai
 Appreciating Wilson, he was quoted as saying, "he was treated like an outcast in school
" apane parivaar kii sthiti se acchhee tarah waakif bejwada ke man main bahut gussa tha lekin unhone baad main apane is gusse kaa istemaal mailaa dhone ke unmoolan kii muhim chalaane main kiya
 "wilson worked for his" movement for 32 years, he not only led the spirit of moral outrage, but also guided the campaign with a great ability to organize and work in India's complex legal system
 did
 ’ "the Board of Trustees selected Bezwada Wilson for the 2016 Ramon Magsaysay Award to give Dalits a proven right to live life with human dignity and to eradicate the humiliating slavery of manual scavenging in India
" Wilson's exceptional skill and moral energy in leading the movement at the level is honored
 ’’ puraskaar ke liye chune gaye ek anya bhartiya 40 varshiya krishna kii prashansa karte hue kaha gaya he ki unhone ‘‘dikhaaya ki sangeet nijee jivan evam samaaj main gaharaa parivartankaree bal ho saktaa he
 Born in a Brahmin family in Chennai, Krishna started training in this genre from the age of six as a teacher of Carnatic music gurus
 unke ullekh main kaha gaya, ‘‘haalanki krishna ne arthshaastra main degree praapt kii, unhone kalakaar bananaa chunaa or jald hi karnataka shastreey sangeet ke ek behtareen kalakaar ke rup main khyaati praapt kar lee
 "it states," The ancient singing and playing music system of Karnataka music started in temples and courts centuries ago, but later it became a predominantly cultural patronage mode of the Brahmin caste, which only those from the elite class Only display or organize or enjoy it which has access to it
 ’’tippaniyan The mention states, "krishna is grateful that Carnatic music shaped his artistry but raised questions on the social basis of this art
" unhone dekha ki unki kala par ek jati vishesh kaa varchasv he or yah kala bharat kii saanskrithik viraasat ke ek ahm hisse main bhagidaari se nichle virgon ko prabhaavshaalee tareeke se baahar karke anyaaypurna vyavastha ko badhaava detii he
 He became the president of the classical music youth association in the 1990s, which took Karnataka music to the youth and government schools

 ' 50 varshiya wilson ke prashansaatmak ullekh main kaha gaya he, ‘‘mailaa dhonaa ek vanshanugat pesha he or 1,80,000 dalit ghar bharat bhar main 7,90,000 saarvajanik evam vyaktigat shushk shauchalayon ko saaf karte hai, mailaa dhone waalon main 98 pratishat mahilaon evam ladakiyon ko bahut maamuli vetan diya jaataa he
 The constitution and other laws ban dry toilets and manual scavenging from people, but they have not been implemented because the government is their biggest violator
 ’’ wilson kaa janm ek aise dalit parivaar main hua jo karnataka ke kolar gold fields kasbe main mailaa dhone kaa kaam karata tha
 He is the first member of his family to receive higher education

 Bezwada, well aware of the situation of his family, was very angry in his mind, but he later used his anger to campaign for the eradication of manual scavenging
 ’’ wilson ne apane ‘‘is andolan ke liye 32 saal kaam kiya, unhone keval naitik aakrosh kii bhaavana kaa hi netritv nahin kiya balki bade paimaane par aayojan karne or bharat kii jatil kanoonee pranali main kaam karne kii shandaar kaabiliyat ke saath muhim kaa maargdarshan kiya
 ' wilson ke ullekh main kaha gaya, ‘‘nyaasiyon ke board ne 2016 reman magasaysay puraskaar ke liye bejwada wilson kaa chayan karke daliton ko maanviya garima ke saath jivan jeene kaa janm siddh adhikaar dilaane or bharat main mailaa dhone kii apmanjanak daastaa ke unmoolan ke liye jamini str par andolan kaa netritv karne main wilson kii asaadhaaran dakshata evam naitik urja ko sammanit kiya he
 Praising another 40-year-old Krishna, who was selected for the award, said that he "showed that music can be a profound transformational force in personal life and society
" ’’ chennai ke brahman parivaar main janme krishna ne karnataka sangeet ke guruon ke sanidhya main chah saal kii aayu se hi is vidha kaa prashikshan lenaa shuru kar diya tha
 He was quoted as saying, "although Krishna received a degree in economics, he chose to become an artist and soon gained a reputation as one of the finest artists of Carnatic classical music
" ’’ isamen kaha gaya he, ‘‘pracheen gayan evam vaadan sangeet pranali karnataka sangeet kaa aarambh sadiyon pehle mandiron evam darbaron main hua tha lekin baad main yah mukhya rup se brahman jati ke saanskrithik sangrakshan vaali vidha ban gai jise keval abhijatya varg ke ve log hi pradarshit yaa yojit karte hai yaa uskaa anand lete hai jinaki is tak pahunch he

 ) The expert team of Pench Tiger Reserve has completed the operation to catch the tiger that has been spreading panic in Seoni, Madhya Pradesh for few days
 trankulij kar pakade gaye baagh ko pinjre main kaidakar sidhi jile main sthit sanjay tigar rigerv main bheja gaya he
 Shubharanjan Sen, area director of Pench Tiger Reserve, said that three elephants were called from Khamaria on Monday to capture Kbagh
 unhone bataaya ki kshetra main dehshat failaa rahe baagh ko pakadaney kii yojana banaakar aaj subah haathiyon kii madad se rescue dal ne baagh ko khamariya gaanv se najadik barghat saamaanya van kshetra ke sandadev raiyat beet ke compatment 165 main gher liya

 ’’ yah kar maang us vivaad main kii gai he jo philhal antarrashtriya panchat main he

 ab ise vodaphone india ke naam se janaa jaataa he

 chidambaram ne saamaanya kar parivarjan rodhi (gaar) niyamon or karadhaan ke niyamon main pichley samay se lagu hone vaale badlaavon jaise maamalon main bhi sanshodhan kaa sanket diya

 pichley aath varsho main se do saalon main dhimaa vikaas hone se hamaara vishwaas kamjor nahin ho saktaa he
 "comments chidambaram ne somvaar ko kaha ki aarthik maamalon kii mantrimandaleey samiti aadharbhoot sanrachana pariyojnaon ko teji se lagu karne ke raste main aane vaali baadhaon ko dur karegi

 " Chidambaram said, “some sectors are under pressure such as petroleum, electricity and textile sectors
 hamen koyala, khanan, petroleum, bijli, sadak parivahan, railway or bandargah kshetra main ucch utpaadan ko baadhit karne vaali samasyaon kaa vyaavhaarik samaadhaan khojna hoga
 " chidambaram ne nivesh main teji laakar vikaas main teji laane kii ek yojana ko saamne rakhaa

 " chidambaram ne kaha ki vishaal nakadi bhandar vaali bhartiya companiyon ko nivesh shuru karne ke liye protsaahit karnaa hoga or videshi nivesh sanvardhan board ke paas aae prastaavon par teji se faisla lenaa hoga
 Chidambaram also indicated amendments in cases such as the General anti-tax Avoidance (GAAR) rules and changes in the rules of taxation which have been in force since time immemorial
 chidambaram ne kaha ki sarkaar jald hi kharche par lagaam lagane or vittiya ghaataa kam karne ke upaay pesh karegi
